     <p> The narrow and winding trails here are on the faces of the cliffs. Carelessness or combat are especially risky here. </p>   The <a class="btn-icon" onclick="javascript:window.app.reroll_ex('YVOe8HfG','City',true);"><i class="fa fa-dice"></i></a>  <a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/location/YVOe8HfG"><strong>City of Headsmen</strong></a> decorates the horizon, surrounded by guarded walls on the edge of the cliffs, at the end of a winding steep trail.
